 The next hearing of the case will also decide whether the petition of Karmaveer Singh is hearable or not

 ipel main jarur piyush ne pratibha kii jhalak dikhaate hue gendbaaji or ballebaaji ke dam par apni team kolkata niterides ko jeet dilaai he
 Special things related to Piyush's cricket career and life
 
 Piyush Chawla was born in Aligarh city of UP
 kam umr main hi daaen haath kii leg spin gendbaaji se unhone apni pahchaan banani shuru kar di
 He made a place in India's Under-19 team and up's Under-21 team at the age of 15
 piyush kaa naam sabase adhik tab media jagat kii surkhiyaan bana jab unhone varsh 2005-06 main master blaster sachin tendulkar ko gugali par bold kiya
 After bowling a cricketer like Sachin, obviously everyone's eye is on you
 thik yahi piyush ke saath hua
 However, in this tournament, the wicket of two other legendary cricketers Mahendra Singh Dhoni and Yuvraj Singh was also a blow by the UP spinner
 mahaj 18 saal kii umr main piyush ne international cricket main apana kariyar shuru kiya
 Played the first Test against England in Mohali in March 2006
 haalanki pehle match main ve koi khaas asar nahin chhod paae
 In the first innings, he bowled 45 runs in nine overs but got no wickets
 haalanki england kii duusari pari main andrew flintaff ko out kar unhone wicket kaa khaataa kholaa
 Piyush made his ODI debut against Bangladesh in May 2007 in Dhaka
 yah match unke liye khaasi safalataa vaala sabit hua or unhone 37 ran dekar teen wicket liye
 He played his first T20 match against South Africa in May 2010 at the Grass Islet (west Indies)
 is match main piyush ne teen over main 27 ran dekar ek wicket hasil kiya tha
 In the IPL, Piyush Chawla played for Kings XI Punjab and then Kolkata Knight Riders from 2008 to 2013
 ipel-7 main kolkata ko champion banane main unhone ahm yogadan diya tha
 The Kolkata team's winning run came off the bat of Piyush itself
 tippaniyan Piyush Chawla was a member of the 2011 World Cup champion Indian team
 haalanki is toornament main unhen keval teen match (netherland, ireland or england ke khilaaf) khilne kaa hi mauka mil paaya tha
 Piyush is also working hard in batting to make a place in Team India again
 kuch samay pehle unhone kaha tha ki aaj cricket itnaa pratispardhaatmak ho gaya he ki nichle kram ke khilaadiyon ke liye bhi ballebaaji ahm banati ja rahi he
 Along with better bowling performance, my focus is also on improving batting

 At the same time, the above items costing more than Rs 1,000 will be taxed at 12 per cent
 resham or jute dhaagaa kochhut shreneemen rakhaa gaya he lekin kapaas or prakritik fibre tathaa anya sabhi dhaagaa par 5 fisadi jiesti lagegaa
 Manmade silk will be taxed at the rate of 18 per cent
 khaadi ko chhodkar anya sabhi shrenee ke kapadon par 5 fisadi kar lagegaa
 Apart from this, Gandhi cap and flag of India will not be taxed under GST
 ek hajaar rupee tak kii laagat vaale maanav nirmit paridhaan par 5 fisadi kar lagegaa jo maujuuda 7 fisadi se kam he
 Those costing more than Rs 1,000 will be taxed at 12 per cent
 iske alaava, maachis, dibbaband jaivik urvarak par nai vyavastha main 5 fisadi kar lagegaa
 The GST Council under the chairmanship of Finance Minister Arun Jaitley has fixed the tax on almost all goods and services
 un vastuon par 5, 12, 18 or 28 fisadi kar lagaaya gaya he

 " dekhen Video: The Delhi Police has arrested three members of a gang stealing luxury vehicles
 giraft main aae in choron ne abhi tak 100 se bhi zyada kaaren churaane kii baat kabool kii he
 Police have recovered 20 vehicles from them
 pakad main aae car choron ke naam anil, shaan or lokesh hai
 All the recovered vehicles were stolen from South Delhi
 pakade jane ke baad teenon ne jokhulasakia wo behad chaunkaane vaala tha
 He said that a new market for vehicles stolen from Delhi has been established in Aligarh, Githore and Moradabad
 yahaan churaai gai gadiyon ke nakli kagajaat taiyaar kiye jate hai
 After which a little change of vehicles is delivered to the market of second-hand vehicles
 yah log kabad main tabdeel ho chuki gaadiyaan bhi kharid lete the taaki chori kii gadiyon ko unke asli kagajaton kaa istemaal kar bech saken
 Police said that one of his companions used to run a garage, where he used to cut the vehicles of Chori and sell their parts
 police ke mutabik, is giroh kaa mastermind arshad naam kaa ek shaks he

 philhal arshad faraar chal rahaa he
 Police are finding out about Arshad's hideouts from the arrested car thieves
 poochtacha main usne sweekaar kiya ki patrkaar rajesh mishra hatyakand main rajeev yadav ke kehane par vah uske saath pulsar motor cycle chalaakar aayaa tha

 badmaash pawan yadav ke paas se ek tamancha, do jinda kaartoos, hatyakand main prayukt motorcycle baraamad kii gai
 The Superintendent of Police has announced a cash prize to the team that caught the prize

 ) Sukma collector Alex Paul Menon's holdings by the Naxalites and talk of his release have not cooled off yet, but in the meantime, some good news came from South Bastar as well
 
 
 jaise - chhattisgarh police ke saath dornapal camp main kaam kar rahe 24 saal ke karti ganga ko pataa chalaa he ki uske pita or bhai ko maovadiyon ne kareeb 15 din tak kaid main rakhane ke baad chhod diya he
 Apart from Karti Ganga, this is also good news for people like 31-year-old Sariyam Bojja, who lives in a nearby village, whose family were picked up by Maoists and suspected of being police informers and assistants
 abhi tak maovadiyon kii ore se reeha gaye ye log apane ghar to nahin pahunche hai, lekin naksaliyon ko ek paigaam safataur par mil rahaa he ki apharan kii is ranneeti main bahut kuch unke khilaaf bhi ja saktaa he
 On visiting this war zone, it is felt that the sympathy of the people living in 'inner' areas is not with the Maoists in this matter
 karti ganga ke pita or bhai ke saath-saath kai duusare gaanvvaalon kii rihaai se lagata he ki maovadi bhi is dabaav ko mahasoos kar rahe hai
 But the abductions done by Maoists do not make a complete picture of the story
 dantewada ke palnar se lage duungarpara gaanv main kai aise log hai, jinke apano ko police ne uthaa liya he
 The 23-year-old's husband was taken away last year by the Special Police Officer (SPO (now the Chhattisgarh government made part of the auxiliary force))
 tab bime garbhvatee thi, or aaj uskaa baccha dedh saal kaa ho chukaa he, lekin pati ab bhi jail main band he
 Hundreds of such stories are buried in the villages of South Bastar
 do saal pehle congress netaa avadhesh gautam ke ghar par maovadiyon ne hamalaa kiya
 The police picked up many people from Dungarpada and adjoining villages on suspicion of being Naxalites, but those languishing in jail are neither being produced in the court nor released from jail
 duungarpara ke paas hi 22 saal ke kosa kii maa gondi bhashaa main jo kuch kahati he, vah to samaj nahin aata, lekin uske lagaataar behate aansu lalpattee main chal rahe dohare aatank kii kahaniyaan saaf sunaate hai
 Her son was also picked up along with Beema's husband, but nothing has been known to her yet
 bharat ke bichombich bani lalpattee par chal rahi is khooni jang main maovadiyon yaa police waalon ko doshi tehraana puure sach se munh chhipaane jaisaa he
 The seed of Salwa Judum, which was sown by the government to eradicate Naxalism in the year 2005, has made the same problem more worsening today
 salwa judum ke daur main mar rahe espeo, police waalon or maovadiyon kii list main ab siarpief ke jawan tezi se jud rahe hai
 Today, landmine blasts are not only killing paramilitary personnel and policemen, but also common people
 dornapal se kuch kilometre aage errabor camp ke halaat or bhi kharaab hai, jahaan naksaliyon ne kai baar hamale kiye hai
 In 2006, when the Salwa Judum was in full force, the Naxalites made a big attack, killed many people and set the camp on fire
 naksal errabor or aasapaas ke ilaakon se police ke kareebi samajhe jane vaale logon kaa apharan bhi karte rahe hai, jinaki kismat kaa faisla maovadiyon ke librated zone main lagane vaali jan adaalaton main hota he
 It is not that everyone is sentenced to death in public courts, because the Naxalites leave some people, whom they feel they will not support the police
 lekin errabor jaise ghor naksalvirohi abhiyaan se jude camp ke logon ke liye aisi ummid kam hoti he
 On the other hand, the hope of justice is extremely blurred for the people rotting in the courts of our country
 sukama or dantewada ke aasapaas bikhare duungarpara, sameli, jabeli, arbeta, kuakonda jaise kai gaanv hai, jahaan logon ko 'apano' ke jail se baahar aane kaa intazaar he
 The plight of these people never becomes a matter of debate in our Parliament thousands of kilometers away, and only reports of Naxalite attacks and government strategy are published in the national media
 jin logon ke naam par 15 se 20 hazaar ardhsainik balon ko jhonkkar yah ladaai ladi ja rahi he, ve yaa to jangal main maovadiyon kii kaid main hai yaa hamaari sabhyataa ke bich bani jelon main sad rahe hai
 The police either defer to the question of innocent people being jailed or they call it propaganda of Maoists, but on the basis of this bitter reality Maoists are preparing their press releases
 is baar bhi naksaliyon ne baqayada bayaan jari kar dm ke apharan ko jaays tehraaya he
 According to him, the DM has ignored the police brutality in his own area and his style of work is going to help the corporate houses
 tippaniyan In their statement, the Naxalites refer to hundreds of villagers who have been thrashed in Dantewada jail or those killed in police custody
 aise main sarkaar ke khilaaf daleel khadi hoti he or netaaon kii vishwasaneeyata kamazor hoti he
 On the other hand, contractors and forest workers have no problem in Bastar forests
 unke haath main blueberi or samsung gallexi ke mobile dikhte hai, jinamein se kai handset main to hispid internet suvidha bhi he
 He advocates for the deployment of strong police officers to control Naxalism in the area, but he does not care for the absence of political visits among the people
 lekin maajhapada – jahaan se sukama ke colector ko agava kiya gaya – main ummid kii ek kiran zarur dikhti he
 The police, who entered the search for the Naxalites after the operation, may have orchestrated the assault, but people still talk of standing with the government
 saaf he ki dm elex paul menon kii mehnat kuch rang zarur laai he
 Will our leaders work to take it forward? 
 
 ? So far, these people who have been released by Maoists have not reached their homes, but the Naxalites are clearly getting a message that in this kidnapping strategy a lot can also go against them
 is war zone kaa daura karne par mahasoos hota he ki 'bhitari' ilaakon main rahane vaale logon kii hamadardi is maamle main maovadiyon ke saath nahin he
 The release of Karti Ganga's father and brother, as well as many other villagers, suggests that the Maoists are also feeling this pressure
 lekin maovadiyon kii ore se kiye gaye apharan kahani kii puri tasviir nahin banaate
 In Dungarpada village adjoining Palanar in Dantewada, there are many people whose people have been picked up by the police
 23 saal kii bime ke pati ko pichley saal special police afasar yani espeo (jinhen ab chhattisgarh sarkaar ne oxilri force kaa hissaa bana diya he) uthaakar le gaye
 Beema was pregnant then, and today her child is one and a half years old, but the husband is still in jail
 aisi saikadon kahaniyaan dakshin bastar ke gaanvon main dabi hui hai
 Two years ago, Maoists attacked the house of Congress leader Awadhesh Gautam
 naksaliyon kaa samarthak hone ke shaq main police ne kai logon ko duungarpara or aasapaas ke gaanvon se uthaaya, lekin jail main sad rahe logon ko na to adaalat main pesh kiya ja rahaa he, na unhen jail se choda rahaa he
 Dungarpada does not understand what she says in Gondi, the mother of 22-year-old Kosa, but her constantly flowing tears tell stories of double terror running in the lalpatti
 uske bete ko bhi bime ke pati ke saath hi uthaa liya gaya, lekin ab tak uskaa kuch pataa nahin chalaa he
 To blame the Maoists or the policemen in this bloody war going on in the middle of India's Lalpatti is like hiding the whole truth
 varsh 2005 main salwa judum kaa jo beej naksalwad ko mitaane ke liye sarkaar ne boyaa, aaj vahi samasya ko or vikaraal bana chukaa he
 Now the list of spos, policemen and Maoists who are dying in the era of Salwa Judum, CRPF personnel are joining fast
 aaj barudi surangon ke dhamaake ardhsainik bal ke javaanon or police ke logon ko hi nahin maar rahe, balki aam log bhi isaki chapet main aa rahe hai
 a few kilometers ahead of Dornapal, the situation in the Errabor camp is worse, where the Naxalites have attacked many times
 varsh 2006 main jab salwa judum zoron par tha to naksaliyon ne ek bada hamalaa kar kai logon ko maar daalaa or camp main aag laga di
 The Naxals have also abducted people considered close to the police from Arrabor and the surrounding areas, whose fate is decided in the mass courts in the Liberated Zone of the Maoists
 aisa nahin he ki jan adaalaton main har kisi ko maut kii sazaa suna di jaati ho, kyonki naksali kuch logon ko chhod bhi dete hai, jinke bare main unhen lagata he ki ve ainda police kaa saath nahin denge
 But such hopes are less for the camp people associated with the extreme anti-naxal operations like Arrabor
 duusari ore hamaare desh kii adaalaton main sad rahe logon ke liye bhi nyaay kii ummid behad dhundhlee he
 Scattered around Sukma and Dantewada are several villages such as Dungarpada, Sameli, Jabeli, Arbetta, Kuakonda, where people are waiting for 'loved ones' to come out of jail
 hazaron kilometre dur hamaari sansad main kabhi in logon kii durdasha bahes kaa mudda nahin banati, or rashtriya media main bhi sirf naksali hamalon or sarkari ranneeti kii khabaren chap rahi hai
 Those who are fighting this battle in the name of 15 to 20 thousand paramilitary forces are either imprisoned by Maoists in the jungle or are rotting in the jails built between our civilization
 begunaah logon ke jail main band hone ke sawaal ko police yaa to taal jaati he yaa phir vah ise maovadiyon kaa prachaar kahati he, lekin isi kadavi hakeekat ke dam par maovadi apane press release taiyaar kar rahe hai
 This time also, Naxalites have issued a statement justifying the abduction of DM
 unke mutabik dm ne apane hi kshetra main pulisia zulm kii andekhi kii he or unki kaaryastylee corporate gharaanon kii madad karne vaali he
 The comments apane bayaan main naksali dantewada kii jail main thuns die gaye saikadon gaanvvaalon kaa zikr karte hai yaa phir police hiraasat main maare gaye logon kaa
 In this case, arguments are raised against the government and the credibility of the leaders is weak
 udhar, bastar ke jangalon main thekedaaron or van karmchaariyon ko koi dikkat nahin hai
 Blackberry and Samsung Galaxy mobiles are visible in their hands, many of which have high speed internet facility
 ve is ilaake main naksalwad ko kaabo karne ke liye kade police afasaron kii tainaati kii vakaalat karte hai, lekin logon ke bich rajanetaaon ke daure na hone kii unhen parvaah nahin he
 But Manjhpada - from where the Sukma Collector was abducted - definitely sees a ray of hope

 An interesting study has revealed that women neither buy perfume for any other woman nor share it with any other woman
 nishkarsh ke mutabik, agar koi mahila kisi parafum ko apane kisi mitra ko de rahi he yaa usase saajha kar rahi he, to nishchit taur par vah parafum use pasand nahin
 According to a study published in the journal 'food Quality and Preference', many women want to keep their choice of perfume a secret because they consider it an integral part of their personal identity
 america ke brigham yang uniwarsity main industrial dizin ke professor tathaa adhyayan ke sah lekhak bryan howell ne kaha, "mahilaon kii pasandida sugandh unki vyaktigat pahchaan kaa mahatvapurn stambh hota he
 " howell ne kaha, "ve ek hi parafum ko varshon tak istemaal karti hai or kuch mahilaayein apane parafum ko apane doston ke bich raaj banaakar rakhti hai
 "comments adhyayan main america va netherlands kii 146 mahilaon par adhyayan kiya gaya
 Howell said, "when women like a perfume, they buy it either for themselves or for their male friend, but not for a female friend
" " According to Howell, "when they don't like a perfume, they buy it neither for themselves nor for their male friend, but for their female friend
" " According to the conclusion, if a woman is giving or sharing a perfume to a friend, then the perfume is definitely not a favorite
 patrika 'food quality and priference' main prakashit ek adhyayan ke mutabik, kai mahilaayein apane pasand ke parafum ko ek raaj rakhana chaahati hai, kyonki ve ise apni vyaktigat pahchaan kaa abhinn hissaa samajhati hai
 Brian Howell, professor of industrial design and co-author of the study at Brigham Young University in the US, said, "women's favorite fragrances are an important pillar of their personal identity
 " Howell said, "they have used the same perfume for years and some women keep their perfumes a secret among their friends
" " tippaniyan The study studied 146 women from the US and the Netherlands
 howell ne kaha, "jab mahilaon ko koi parafum pasand aata he, to ve use yaa to apane liye kharidti hai yaa apane purush mitra ke liye, lekin kisi mahila mitra ke liye nahin
 " howell ke mutabik, "jab unhen koi parafum pasand nahin aata, to ve ise na to apane liye or na hi apane purush mitra ke liye, balki apni mahila mitra ke liye kharidti hai
 " patrika 'food quality and priference' main prakashit ek adhyayan ke mutabik, kai mahilaayein apane pasand ke parafum ko ek raaj rakhana chaahati hai, kyonki ve ise apni vyaktigat pahchaan kaa abhinn hissaa samajhati hai
